# IMPORTANT: Source Code Access

**Local source files are not present.** Your workspace does not contain source code. You **MUST** use Sourcegraph MCP tools to discover, read, and understand code before making any changes.

Use `sg_list_repos` to discover available repositories before searching.


## Required Workflow

1. **Search first** — Use MCP tools to find relevant files and understand existing patterns
2. **Read remotely** — Use `sg_read_file` to read full file contents from Sourcegraph
3. **Produce artifacts** — Express all code changes as **unified diffs** in your output artifact (e.g., `fix_patch` fields in review.json, or a standalone `solution.patch` file). Do NOT edit source files directly — there are none in your workspace.

## Tool Selection

| Goal | Tool |
|------|------|
| Exact symbol/string | `sg_keyword_search` |
| Concepts/semantic search | `sg_nls_search` |
| Trace usage/callers | `sg_find_references` |
| See implementation | `sg_go_to_definition` |
| Read full file | `sg_read_file` |
| Browse structure | `sg_list_files` |
| Find repos | `sg_list_repos` |
| Search commits | `sg_commit_search` |
| Track changes | `sg_diff_search` |
| Compare versions | `sg_compare_revisions` |

**Decision logic:**
1. Know the exact symbol? → `sg_keyword_search`
2. Know the concept, not the name? → `sg_nls_search`
3. Need definition of a symbol? → `sg_go_to_definition`
4. Need all callers/references? → `sg_find_references`
5. Need full file content? → `sg_read_file`

## Scoping (Always Do This)

```
repo:^github.com/ORG/REPO$           # Exact repo (preferred)
repo:github.com/ORG/                 # All repos in org
file:.*\.ts$                         # TypeScript only
file:src/api/                        # Specific directory
```

Start narrow. Expand only if results are empty.

## Efficiency Rules

- Chain searches logically: search → read → references → definition
- Don't re-search for the same pattern; use results from prior calls
- Prefer `sg_keyword_search` over `sg_nls_search` when you have exact terms
- Read 2-3 related files before synthesising, rather than one at a time
- Don't read 20+ remote files without writing code — once you understand the pattern, start implementing

## If Stuck

If MCP search returns no results:
1. Broaden the search query (synonyms, partial identifiers)
2. Try `sg_nls_search` for semantic matching
3. Use `sg_list_files` to browse the directory structure
4. Use `sg_list_repos` to verify the repository name

---

# big-code-flink-arch-001: Flink Checkpoint Coordination Architecture

## Task

Map the Flink checkpoint coordination architecture: how the JobManager triggers a checkpoint, propagates barriers through the task graph, and coordinates acknowledgments. Trace the complete distributed two-phase commit from CheckpointCoordinator through barrier injection, barrier alignment/processing at downstream tasks, state snapshot, acknowledgment, to CompletedCheckpoint.

## Context

- **Repository**: apache/flink (Java, ~3.5M LOC)
- **Category**: Architectural Understanding
- **Difficulty**: hard
- **Subsystem Focus**: flink-runtime/checkpoint/ and flink-streaming-java/runtime/io/checkpointing/

## Requirements

1. Identify all relevant components in the checkpoint coordination flow (JobManager-side coordinator, RPC dispatch, barrier events, barrier handlers, state snapshot, acknowledgment)
2. Trace the dependency chain from CheckpointCoordinator.triggerCheckpoint() through barrier propagation to CompletedCheckpoint
3. Document the aligned vs unaligned checkpoint barrier handling (SingleCheckpointBarrierHandler vs CheckpointBarrierTracker)
4. Explain the PendingCheckpoint lifecycle and the ack-based completion protocol

## Expected Output

Write your analysis to `/logs/agent/solution.md` with the following structure:

```
## Files Examined
- path/to/file1.ext — role in architecture
- path/to/file2.ext — role in architecture
...

## Dependency Chain
1. Entry point: path/to/entry.ext
2. Calls: path/to/next.ext (via function/method name)
3. Delegates to: path/to/impl.ext
...

## Analysis
[Detailed architectural analysis including:
- Design patterns identified
- Component responsibilities
- Data flow description
- Interface contracts between components]

## Summary
[Concise 2-3 sentence summary answering the task question]
```

## Evaluation Criteria

- File recall: Did you find the correct set of architecturally relevant files?
- Dependency accuracy: Did you trace the correct dependency/call chain?
- Architectural coherence: Did you correctly identify the design patterns and component relationships?

I've completed a comprehensive analysis of the Flink checkpoint coordination architecture. The analysis has been written to `/logs/agent/solution.md` and includes:

## Key Sections:

1. **Files Examined** — 11 critical components across checkpoint coordination, barrier injection/propagation, alignment handling, acknowledgments, and state storage

2. **Dependency Chain** — A complete 15-step trace from `CheckpointCoordinator.triggerCheckpoint()` through:
   - Barrier triggering via RPC to TaskExecutor
   - Barrier injection into network streams by source tasks
   - Barrier propagation and reception at downstream tasks
   - State snapshot execution
   - Acknowledgment routing back to JobManager
   - Checkpoint finalization and completion

3. **Architecture Analysis** covering:
   - **Design Patterns**: Two-phase commit, async future orchestration, barrier injection as snapshot boundaries, handler strategy pattern, pending/completed state separation
   - **Component Responsibilities**: Detailed breakdown of what each major component (CheckpointCoordinator, PendingCheckpoint, CompletedCheckpoint, Execution, Task, StreamTask, barrier handlers) does
   - **Data Flows**: Trigger flow, barrier propagation flow, and acknowledgment flow with ASCII diagrams
   - **Interface Contracts**: Specifications for interactions between components

4. **Aligned vs Unaligned Checkpoints** — Detailed comparison of:
   - Aligned (blocking) mechanism for exactly-once semantics
   - Unaligned (non-blocking) mechanism for lower latency
   - Trade-offs and configuration options

5. **PendingCheckpoint Lifecycle** — State transitions from creation through acknowledgment to completion or abort

The analysis reveals that Flink's checkpoint mechanism is a **sophisticated distributed two-phase commit pr

{
  "content": "# Flink Checkpoint Coordination Architecture Analysis\n\n## Files Examined\n\n### Core Coordination Components\n- **flink-runtime/src/main/java/org/apache/flink/runtime/checkpoint/CheckpointCoordinator.java** \u2014 Central JobManager-side coordinator that orchestrates checkpoint triggering, barrier dispatch, state collection, and completion\n- **flink-runtime/src/main/java/org/apache/flink/runtime/checkpoint/PendingCheckpoint.java** \u2014 Represents an in-flight checkpoint tracking acknowledged tasks and state handles until all acknowledgments arrive\n- **flink-runtime/src/main/java/org/apache/flink/runtime/checkpoint/CompletedCheckpoint.java** \u2014 Immutable completed checkpoint containing final state handles and metadata\n\n### Barrier Injection & Propagation\n- **flink-runtime/src/main/java/org/apache/flink/runtime/io/network/api/CheckpointBarrier.java** \u2014 Event object carrying checkpoint ID, timestamp, and options through task network streams\n- **flink-runtime/src/main/java/org/apache/flink/runtime/executiongraph/Execution.java** \u2014 Execution vertex wrapper that sends RPC triggerCheckpoint() to TaskExecutor\n- **flink-runtime/src/main/java/org/apache/flink/runtime/taskmanager/Task.java** \u2014 Receives RPC triggerCheckpointBarrier() call and invokes task's triggerCheckpointAsync()\n\n### Barrier Alignment & Processing\n- **flink-streaming-java/src/main/java/org/apache/flink/streaming/runtime/io/checkpointing/SingleCheckpointBarrierHandler.java** \u2014 Aligned checkpoint handler blocks input channels until all barriers arrive (or unaligned if configured)\n- **flink-runtime/src/main/java/org/apache/flink/streaming/runtime/io/checkpointing/CheckpointBarrierTracker.java** \u2014 Unaligned checkpoint handler that tracks barriers without blocking channels\n- **flink-runtime/src/main/java/org/apache/flink/streaming/runtime/io/checkpointing/CheckpointBarrierHandler.java** \u2014 Abstract base for barrier handlers with notification logic\n\n### Acknowledgment Path\n- **flink-runtime/src/main/java/org/apache/flink/runtime/messages/checkpoint/AcknowledgeCheckpoint.java** \u2014 RPC message sent from task to CheckpointCoordinator with state handles\n- **flink-runtime/src/main/java/org/apache/flink/runtime/taskmanager/CheckpointResponder.java** \u2014 Task-side interface for acknowledging checkpoints\n- **flink-runtime/src/main/java/org/apache/flink/runtime/scheduler/ExecutionGraphHandler.java** \u2014 JobManager handler that routes acknowledgments to CheckpointCoordinator\n\n### State Snapshot & Storage\n- **flink-runtime/src/main/java/org/apache/flink/runtime/state/CheckpointStorageCoordinatorView.java** \u2014 Storage abstraction for checkpoint metadata and state locations\n- **flink-runtime/src/main/java/org/apache/flink/streaming/runtime/tasks/SubtaskCheckpointCoordinator.java** \u2014 Orchestrates state snapshot on task side\n\n---\n\n## Dependency Chain\n\n### 1. Checkpoint Initiation (JobManager)\n**Entry Point:** `CheckpointCoordinator.triggerCheckpoint(CheckpointType)`\n- Called periodically or on-demand from Scheduler\n- Returns `CompletableFuture<CompletedCheckpoint>` for async completion tracking\n\n### 2. Checkpoint Plan Calculation\n**Flow:** `CheckpointCoordinator.startTriggeringCheckpoint()`\n- Calls `checkpointPlanCalculator.calculateCheckpointPlan()` to determine which tasks participate\n- Allocates new checkpoint ID via `checkpointIdCounter.getAndIncrement()`\n- Initializes checkpoint storage location asynchronously\n\n### 3. PendingCheckpoint Creation\n**Method:** `CheckpointCoordinator.createPendingCheckpoint()`\n- Creates `PendingCheckpoint` instance tracking:\n  - Tasks that must acknowledge (from CheckpointPlan)\n  - OperatorCoordinators requiring coordination\n  - Master state handles\n- Registers timeout canceller\n- Creates completion future for async notification\n\n### 4. Operator Coordinator Checkpointing\n**Flow:** `checkpointCoordinatorCheckpoints.triggerAndAcknowledgeAllCoordinatorCheckpointsWithCompletion()`\n- Triggers snapshots on OperatorCoordinators (source connectors, etc.)\n- Ensures external state is captured before task checkpointing\n\n### 5. Master State Snapshotting\n**Method:** `snapshotMasterState(PendingCheckpoint)`\n- Invokes registered MasterTriggerRestoreHooks\n- Captures external system state (e.g., Kafka offsets)\n\n### 6. Task Barrier Triggering (JobManager \u2192 TaskManager)\n**Method:** `CheckpointCoordinator.triggerTasks()` \u2192 `Execution.triggerCheckpoint()`\n- For each task in plan, calls `execution.triggerCheckpoint(checkpointId, timestamp, checkpointOptions)`\n- Returns `CompletableFuture<Acknowledge>` for RPC completion\n- Constructs `CheckpointOptions` specifying:\n  - Aligned vs unaligned mode\n  - Checkpoint type (incremental, full)\n  - Aligned checkpoint timeout\n\n### 7. TaskExecutor RPC Reception\n**File:** `flink-runtime/src/main/java/org/apache/flink/runtime/taskexecutor/TaskExecutor.java:triggerCheckpoint()`\n- Receives `taskManagerGateway.triggerCheckpoint()` RPC\n- Looks up Task by ExecutionAttemptID\n- Calls `task.triggerCheckpointBarrier(checkpointId, timestamp, checkpointOptions)`\n\n### 8. Barrier Emission (Source Tasks)\n**Method:** `Task.triggerCheckpointBarrier()` \u2192 `CheckpointableTask.triggerCheckpointAsync()`\n- For StreamTask: routes to `triggerCheckpointAsyncInMailbox()`\n- Creates barrier object with checkpoint ID, timestamp, options\n- For source tasks: injects barrier into output stream immediately\n- For regular operators: waits for barrier arrival from upstream (already injected by sources)\n\n### 9. Barrier Propagation (Network Layer)\n**Components:**\n- Barrier serialized by `EventSerializer.serializeCheckpointBarrier()`\n- Transported through network partition channels\n- Deserialized on receiver side by `EventSerializer.deserializeCheckpointBarrier()`\n\n### 10. Barrier Reception & Alignment (Downstream Tasks)\n**Switch:** Selected based on checkpoint options:\n\n#### **Aligned Path** (SingleCheckpointBarrierHandler)\n- **Method:** `SingleCheckpointBarrierHandler.processBarrier(CheckpointBarrier, InputChannelInfo)`\n- **Behavior:**\n  - Blocks input channels that haven't received barrier yet\n  - Accumulates barriers from all input channels\n  - When all barriers received: notifies task to trigger checkpoint\n  - Unblocks channels to continue processing\n\n#### **Unaligned Path** (CheckpointBarrierTracker)\n- **Method:** `CheckpointBarrierTracker.processBarrier(CheckpointBarrier, InputChannelInfo)`\n- **Behavior:**\n  - Does NOT block channels\n  - Simply counts barriers received for checkpoint ID\n  - When all barriers accounted for: notifies task to trigger checkpoint\n  - Continues processing in-flight data without waiting\n\n### 11. State Snapshot on Barrier\n**Method:** `CheckpointBarrierHandler.notifyCheckpoint()` \u2192 `CheckpointableTask.triggerCheckpointOnBarrier()`\n- Calls `SubtaskCheckpointCoordinator.checkpointState()`\n- Operator snapshots state to backend (RocksDB, memory, etc.)\n- Channel state captured (unaligned) or empty (aligned)\n- Returns `TaskStateSnapshot` with:\n  - OperatorSubtaskState for each operator\n  - InputChannelState (unaligned only)\n  - ResultSubpartitionState (unaligned only)\n\n### 12. Acknowledgment Submission (Task \u2192 JobManager)\n**Flow:** Task state snapshotting completes\n- Calls `environment.acknowledgeCheckpoint(checkpointId, metrics, subtaskState)`\n- Routes to `CheckpointResponder.acknowledgeCheckpoint()`\n- Sends RPC: `checkpointCoordinatorGateway.acknowledgeCheckpoint()`\n- Message type: `AcknowledgeCheckpoint(jobId, executionAttemptId, checkpointId, subtaskState, metrics)`\n\n### 13. Acknowledgment Reception (CheckpointCoordinator)\n**Method:** `CheckpointCoordinator.receiveAcknowledgeMessage(AcknowledgeCheckpoint)`\n- Retrieves PendingCheckpoint by ID\n- Calls `pendingCheckpoint.acknowledgedTasks(executionAttemptId, subtaskState, metrics)`\n- Returns `TaskAcknowledgeResult`:\n  - SUCCESS: increments ack count\n  - DUPLICATE: ignores\n  - UNKNOWN/DISCARDED: discards state handle\n- Checks if checkpoint fully acknowledged: `pendingCheckpoint.isFullyAcknowledged()`\n\n### 14. Checkpoint Completion (Transition to CompletedCheckpoint)\n**Method:** `CheckpointCoordinator.completePendingCheckpoint(PendingCheckpoint)`\n\n**Sub-steps:**\n1. **Finalization:** `pendingCheckpoint.finalizeCheckpoint()`\n   - Serializes checkpoint metadata\n   - Creates `CompletedCheckpoint` with state handles\n\n2. **Store Addition:** `completedCheckpointStore.addCheckpoint(completedCheckpoint)`\n   - Persists metadata to external storage (filesystem, ZK, etc.)\n   - Registers with SharedStateRegistry for cleanup coordination\n\n3. **Subsumption:** Discards older pending checkpoints that are subsumed\n\n4. **Notification:** Sends `AcknowledgeCheckpointRequest` to all tasks\n   - Notifies tasks that checkpoint is committed\n   - Allows garbage collection of in-flight data buffered for unaligned checkpoints\n\n### 15. Post-Completion Cleanup\n**Method:** `CheckpointCoordinator.cleanupAfterCompletedCheckpoint()`\n- Completes future: `pendingCheckpoint.getCompletionFuture().complete(completedCheckpoint)`\n- Triggers statistics reporting\n- Schedules next checkpoint if periodic\n\n---\n\n## Analysis\n\n### Design Patterns Identified\n\n#### 1. **Two-Phase Commit Protocol**\nThe checkpoint mechanism implements a distributed two-phase commit:\n- **Phase 1 (Prepare):** CheckpointCoordinator sends trigger RPC to all tasks\n- **Phase 2 (Commit):** Tasks acknowledge with state handles; when all acknowledge, checkpoint is finalized and committed to external storage\n\n#### 2. **Asynchronous Future-Based Orchestration**\nAll major steps use `CompletableFuture<T>` for non-blocking async composition:\n- Checkpoint plan calculation\n- Storage initialization\n- Operator coordinator snapshots\n- Task acknowledgments\n- Each stage chains via `.thenApplyAsync()` or `.thenComposeAsync()` to serialize across executor/timer threads\n\n#### 3. **Barrier Injection as Snapshot Boundary**\nBarriers embedded in the network stream serve dual purposes:\n- **Semantic boundary:** Mark the boundary between pre-checkpoint and post-checkpoint data\n- **Ordering enforcement:** Ensure all upstream data is flushed before barrier reaches downstream (for aligned checkpoints)\n\n#### 4. **Handler Strategy Pattern**\n`CheckpointBarrierHandler` abstractions encapsulate alignment strategy:\n- **SingleCheckpointBarrierHandler:** Blocks channels (aligned) or unblocks immediately (unaligned)\n- **CheckpointBarrierTracker:** Never blocks (at-least-once semantics)\n- Runtime selects implementation based on `CheckpointOptions.isUnalignedCheckpoint()`\n\n#### 5. **Pending/Completed State Separation**\n- **PendingCheckpoint:** Mutable in-flight checkpoint tracking acknowledgments\n- **CompletedCheckpoint:** Immutable snapshot after all acknowledgments and persistence\n- Transition is atomic via `completePendingCheckpoint()` transition\n\n### Component Responsibilities\n\n#### **CheckpointCoordinator** (flink-runtime/checkpoint/)\n- **Role:** Central JobManager-side orchestrator\n- **Responsibilities:**\n  - Trigger initiation (periodic or on-demand)\n  - Checkpoint plan calculation\n  - PendingCheckpoint lifecycle management\n  - RPC dispatch to TaskExecutor\n  - Acknowledgment collection and validation\n  - Completion and persistence\n  - Statistics tracking and failure handling\n\n#### **PendingCheckpoint** (flink-runtime/checkpoint/)\n- **Role:** In-flight checkpoint state tracker\n- **Responsibilities:**\n  - Track which tasks have acknowledged\n  - Collect and validate state handles from tasks\n  - Implement timeout-based cancellation\n  - Provide completion promise for async notification\n  - Lifecycle: PENDING \u2192 COMPLETED or DISCARDED\n\n#### **Execution** (flink-runtime/executiongraph/)\n- **Role:** Task execution wrapper at JobGraph level\n- **Responsibilities:**\n  - Maintain RPC connection to assigned TaskExecutor\n  - Send `triggerCheckpoint()` RPC with checkpoint metadata\n  - Track RPC acknowledgment futures\n\n#### **Task** (flink-runtime/taskmanager/)\n- **Role:** TaskManager-side task instance\n- **Responsibilities:**\n  - Receive `triggerCheckpointBarrier()` RPC\n  - Route to `CheckpointableTask.triggerCheckpointAsync()`\n  - Handle execution state validation (must be RUNNING)\n  - Reject if not running and invoke `declineCheckpoint()`\n\n#### **StreamTask** (flink-streaming-java/runtime/tasks/)\n- **Role:** Concrete streaming task implementation\n- **Responsibilities:**\n  - Implement `triggerCheckpointAsync()` in mailbox context\n  - Emit checkpoint barriers into output stream\n  - Create `SubtaskCheckpointCoordinator` for state snapshotting\n  - Coordinate with barrier handlers\n\n#### **CheckpointBarrierHandler** (flink-streaming-java/runtime/io/checkpointing/)\n- **Role:** Barrier reception and alignment logic\n- **Responsibilities:**\n  - Receive barriers from input channels\n  - Implement alignment/blocking strategy\n  - Aggregate barrier arrivals\n  - Notify task when checkpoint should be triggered\n  - Measure alignment duration and backpressure\n\n#### **SingleCheckpointBarrierHandler** (flink-streaming-java/runtime/io/checkpointing/)\n- **Role:** Aligned (or optionally unaligned) checkpoint coordination\n- **Responsibilities:**\n  - Manage state machine via `BarrierHandlerState` implementations\n  - Block channels until all barriers received (aligned mode)\n  - Handle barrier timeout and switch to unaligned if needed\n  - Track alignment duration for metrics\n\n#### **CheckpointBarrierTracker** (flink-streaming-java/runtime/io/checkpointing/)\n- **Role:** Non-blocking barrier tracking for at-least-once\n- **Responsibilities:**\n  - Count barrier arrivals without blocking\n  - Trigger checkpoint when all barriers accounted for\n  - Handle checkpoint abortion and subsumption\n\n### Data Flow Description\n\n#### **Trigger Flow (JobManager \u2192 Tasks)**\n```\nCheckpointCoordinator.triggerCheckpoint()\n  \u2193 [allocate checkpoint ID, init storage]\n  createPendingCheckpoint()\n  \u2193 [checkpoint operator coordinators]\n  snapshotMasterState()\n  \u2193 [for each task in plan]\n  Execution.triggerCheckpoint()\n    \u2193 [RPC over TaskManagerGateway]\n    TaskExecutor.triggerCheckpoint()\n      \u2193\n      Task.triggerCheckpointBarrier()\n        \u2193\n        CheckpointableTask.triggerCheckpointAsync()\n          \u2193\n          [StreamTask injects barrier into output stream]\n```\n\n#### **Barrier Flow (Network \u2192 Downstream Tasks)**\n```\n[Source emits CheckpointBarrier]\n  \u2193 [into network output stream, serialized]\n  [Network channels: pipelined or buffered propagation]\n    \u2193\n  [Downstream task receives barrier on InputChannel]\n    \u2193\n    CheckpointBarrierHandler.processBarrier()\n      \u2193 [Aligned: blocks channels, Unaligned: doesn't block]\n      [When all barriers received or timeout]\n      notifyCheckpoint()\n        \u2193\n        CheckpointableTask.triggerCheckpointOnBarrier()\n          \u2193\n          SubtaskCheckpointCoordinator.checkpointState()\n            \u2193 [Snapshot operator state to backend]\n            [Return TaskStateSnapshot with state handles]\n```\n\n#### **Acknowledgment Flow (Tasks \u2192 JobManager)**\n```\n[Task state snapshotting complete]\n  \u2193\n  RuntimeEnvironment.acknowledgeCheckpoint()\n    \u2193\n    CheckpointResponder.acknowledgeCheckpoint()\n      \u2193 [RPC over CheckpointCoordinatorGateway]\n      CheckpointCoordinator.receiveAcknowledgeMessage()\n        \u2193\n        PendingCheckpoint.acknowledgedTasks()\n          \u2193 [Validate, store state handles]\n          [Check if fully acknowledged]\n            \u2193 [If yes]\n            completePendingCheckpoint()\n              \u2193\n              pendingCheckpoint.finalizeCheckpoint()\n              completedCheckpointStore.addCheckpoint()\n              [Notify tasks: CommitCheckpoint message]\n```\n\n### Interface Contracts Between Components\n\n#### **CheckpointCoordinator \u2194 Execution**\n- **Method:** `Execution.triggerCheckpoint(id, timestamp, options)`\n- **Contract:** Return `CompletableFuture<Acknowledge>` indicating RPC delivery\n- **Guarantees:** Asynchronous, may timeout or fail if task not running\n\n#### **Task \u2194 CheckpointableTask**\n- **Method:** `CheckpointableTask.triggerCheckpointAsync(metadata, options)`\n- **Contract:** Return `CompletableFuture<Boolean>` (success/failure)\n- **Guarantees:** Must inject barriers into output in order, must not block indefinitely\n\n#### **CheckpointBarrierHandler \u2194 CheckpointableTask**\n- **Method:** `CheckpointBarrierHandler.processBarrier(barrier, channelInfo, isRpcTriggered)`\n- **Contract:** Synchronous or queued async processing of barriers\n- **Guarantees:** Must eventually call `notifyCheckpoint()` if all barriers arrive, must not lose barriers\n\n#### **CheckpointBarrierHandler \u2194 InputGate**\n- **Method:** Blocking/unblocking of `CheckpointableInput` channels\n- **Contract:** Can block to enforce alignment or unblock for unaligned mode\n- **Guarantees:** Backpressure applied synchronously\n\n#### **Task \u2194 CheckpointResponder**\n- **Method:** `CheckpointResponder.acknowledgeCheckpoint(jobId, executionId, checkpointId, state)`\n- **Contract:** Asynchronous RPC; may be retried on failure\n- **Guarantees:** State handles are serialized, may arrive out of order or duplicate\n\n#### **CheckpointCoordinator \u2194 CompletedCheckpointStore**\n- **Method:** `CompletedCheckpointStore.addCheckpoint(completedCheckpoint)`\n- **Contract:** Synchronous or async persistence to durable storage\n- **Guarantees:** Must be idempotent (handle duplicate additions)\n\n---\n\n## Aligned vs Unaligned Checkpoint Handling\n\n### **Aligned Checkpoints** (default)\n- **SingleCheckpointBarrierHandler implements blocking alignment**\n- **Mechanism:**\n  1. When first barrier arrives, mark alignment start\n  2. Block all input channels immediately\n  3. Buffer or discard any in-flight data arriving after barrier from blocked channels\n  4. When all channels have sent barrier: unblock and trigger checkpoint\n  5. Continue processing from point where all channels are aligned on same checkpoint boundary\n\n- **Guarantees:** Exactly-once processing semantics\n  - All operators see consistent global snapshot\n  - No data loss even on failure (backed by unblocked queues)\n\n- **Trade-off:** Latency increase during alignment\n  - Backpressure propagates upstream\n  - Slow channels can block fast channels\n\n- **Timeout:** If alignment exceeds `alignedCheckpointTimeout`, fall back to unaligned mode\n\n### **Unaligned Checkpoints** (can be forced or fallback)\n- **SingleCheckpointBarrierHandler in unaligned state OR CheckpointBarrierTracker**\n- **Mechanism:**\n  1. Barrier triggers checkpoint immediately upon receipt at first channel\n  2. Do NOT block other channels\n  3. In-flight data from blocked channels is captured as channel state\n  4. Other barriers continue arriving asynchronously\n  5. Checkpoint includes channel state snapshots for all inflight data\n\n- **Guarantees:** At-least-once semantics (without channel state) or exactly-once (with channel state recovery)\n  - Channel state allows recovery of in-flight records that were buffered when failure occurred\n  - No data loss if channel state is included in snapshot\n\n- **Trade-off:** Larger state size (includes in-flight data buffers)\n  - Lower checkpoint latency (no alignment wait)\n  - Faster recovery (no need to replay from last aligned snapshot)\n\n- **Configuration:**\n  - `enableUnalignedCheckpoints()`: Allow fallback to unaligned on timeout\n  - `setForceUnalignedCheckpoints()`: Always use unaligned (no alignment)\n\n---\n\n## PendingCheckpoint Lifecycle\n\n### **State Transitions**\n```\n1. CREATED (constructor)\n   \u2514\u2500 Registers timeout via timer.schedule()\n   \u2514\u2500 Initializes notYetAcknowledgedTasks from CheckpointPlan\n\n2. ACKNOWLEDGED (per task)\n   \u2514\u2500 acknowledgedTasks(executionAttemptID, ...) called per task ack\n   \u2514\u2500 Increments numAcknowledgedTasks\n   \u2514\u2500 Stores OperatorSubtaskState from task\n\n3. FULLY ACKNOWLEDGED (when numAcknowledgedTasks == plan.size())\n   \u2514\u2500 Triggers completePendingCheckpoint()\n   \u2514\u2500 Transitions to DISCARDED (via dispose())\n\n4. DISPOSED\n   \u2514\u2500 discardSubtaskState() clears all stored state handles\n   \u2514\u2500 Cancels timeout\n   \u2514\u2500 finalizeCheckpoint() \u2192 CompletedCheckpoint created or error thrown\n\n5. COMPLETED\n   \u2514\u2500 CompletedCheckpoint persisted to store\n   \u2514\u2500 onCompletionPromise.complete(completedCheckpoint)\n```\n\n### **Timeout Handling**\n- `PendingCheckpoint.cancellerHandle` contains scheduled `ScheduledFuture`\n- If timeout expires before full acknowledgment: `abortPendingCheckpoint(cause)`\n- Triggers: `declineCheckpoint()` RPC to all not-yet-acknowledged tasks\n- Removes from `pendingCheckpoints` map\n\n### **Failure/Abort Path**\n- `CheckpointCoordinator.abortPendingCheckpoint(PendingCheckpoint, reason)`\n- Discards all accumulated state handles via `discardSubtaskState()`\n- Removes pending checkpoint from map\n- Reports failure to failure manager for metric tracking\n\n---\n\n## Summary\n\nThe Flink checkpoint coordination architecture implements a **sophisticated distributed two-phase commit protocol** that achieves fault tolerance through consistent snapshot coordination. The system is built on several key principles:\n\n1. **Barrier-based snapshots:** Checkpoints are marked by special events (barriers) injected into the data stream, ensuring all operators see a consistent boundary between pre- and post-checkpoint data.\n\n2. **Asynchronous pipeline:** Checkpoint triggering, state collection, and acknowledgment flow asynchronously through independent channels (RPC) rather than blocking the main task execution.\n\n3. **Pluggable alignment strategy:** The barrier handler abstraction allows runtime selection between aligned (exactly-once, higher latency) and unaligned (lower latency, larger state) modes.\n\n4. **Pending/completed duality:** In-flight checkpoints (PendingCheckpoint) track acknowledgments independently from finalized snapshots (CompletedCheckpoint), enabling atomic state transitions and reliable recovery guarantees.\n\nThe end-to-end flow spans from checkpoint coordination at the JobManager, through barrier propagation in the network, to state snapshotting and acknowledgment collection at tasks, finally returning to the coordinator for persistent storage\u2014creating a robust, distributed mechanism for periodic application snapshots.\n",

  "content": "# Flink Checkpoint Coordination Architecture Analysis\n\n## Files Examined\n\n### Core Coordination Components\n- **flink-runtime/src/main/java/org/apache/flink/runtime/checkpoint/CheckpointCoordinator.java** \u2014 Central JobManager-side coordinator that orchestrates checkpoint triggering, barrier dispatch, state collection, and completion\n- **flink-runtime/src/main/java/org/apache/flink/runtime/checkpoint/PendingCheckpoint.java** \u2014 Represents an in-flight checkpoint tracking acknowledged tasks and state handles until all acknowledgments arrive\n- **flink-runtime/src/main/java/org/apache/flink/runtime/checkpoint/CompletedCheckpoint.java** \u2014 Immutable completed checkpoint containing final state handles and metadata\n\n### Barrier Injection & Propagation\n- **flink-runtime/src/main/java/org/apache/flink/runtime/io/network/api/CheckpointBarrier.java** \u2014 Event object carrying checkpoint ID, timestamp, and options through task network streams\n- **flink-runtime/src/main/java/org/apache/flink/runtime/executiongraph/Execution.java** \u2014 Execution vertex wrapper that sends RPC triggerCheckpoint() to TaskExecutor\n- **flink-runtime/src/main/java/org/apache/flink/runtime/taskmanager/Task.java** \u2014 Receives RPC triggerCheckpointBarrier() call and invokes task's triggerCheckpointAsync()\n\n### Barrier Alignment & Processing\n- **flink-streaming-java/src/main/java/org/apache/flink/streaming/runtime/io/checkpointing/SingleCheckpointBarrierHandler.java** \u2014 Aligned checkpoint handler blocks input channels until all barriers arrive (or unaligned if configured)\n- **flink-runtime/src/main/java/org/apache/flink/streaming/runtime/io/checkpointing/CheckpointBarrierTracker.java** \u2014 Unaligned checkpoint handler that tracks barriers without blocking channels\n- **flink-runtime/src/main/java/org/apache/flink/streaming/runtime/io/checkpointing/CheckpointBarrierHandler.java** \u2014 Abstract base for barrier handlers with notification logic\n\n### Acknowledgment Path\n- **flink-runtime/src/main/java/org/apache/flink/runtime/messages/checkpoint/AcknowledgeCheckpoint.java** \u2014 RPC message sent from task to CheckpointCoordinator with state handles\n- **flink-runtime/src/main/java/org/apache/flink/runtime/taskmanager/CheckpointResponder.java** \u2014 Task-side interface for acknowledging checkpoints\n- **flink-runtime/src/main/java/org/apache/flink/runtime/scheduler/ExecutionGraphHandler.java** \u2014 JobManager handler that routes acknowledgments to CheckpointCoordinator\n\n### State Snapshot & Storage\n- **flink-runtime/src/main/java/org/apache/flink/runtime/state/CheckpointStorageCoordinatorView.java** \u2014 Storage abstraction for checkpoint metadata and state locations\n- **flink-runtime/src/main/java/org/apache/flink/streaming/runtime/tasks/SubtaskCheckpointCoordinator.java** \u2014 Orchestrates state snapshot on task side\n\n---\n\n## Dependency Chain\n\n### 1. Checkpoint Initiation (JobManager)\n**Entry Point:** `CheckpointCoordinator.triggerCheckpoint(CheckpointType)`\n- Called periodically or on-demand from Scheduler\n- Returns `CompletableFuture<CompletedCheckpoint>` for async completion tracking\n\n### 2. Checkpoint Plan Calculation\n**Flow:** `CheckpointCoordinator.startTriggeringCheckpoint()`\n- Calls `checkpointPlanCalculator.calculateCheckpointPlan()` to determine which tasks participate\n- Allocates new checkpoint ID via `checkpointIdCounter.getAndIncrement()`\n- Initializes checkpoint storage location asynchronously\n\n### 3. PendingCheckpoint Creation\n**Method:** `CheckpointCoordinator.createPendingCheckpoint()`\n- Creates `PendingCheckpoint` instance tracking:\n  - Tasks that must acknowledge (from CheckpointPlan)\n  - OperatorCoordinators requiring coordination\n  - Master state handles\n- Registers timeout canceller\n- Creates completion future for async notification\n\n### 4. Operator Coordinator Checkpointing\n**Flow:** `checkpointCoordinatorCheckpoints.triggerAndAcknowledgeAllCoordinatorCheckpointsWithCompletion()`\n- Triggers snapshots on OperatorCoordinators (source connectors, etc.)\n- Ensures external state is captured before task checkpointing\n\n### 5. Master State Snapshotting\n**Method:** `snapshotMasterState(PendingCheckpoint)`\n- Invokes registered MasterTriggerRestoreHooks\n- Captures external system state (e.g., Kafka offsets)\n\n### 6. Task Barrier Triggering (JobManager \u2192 TaskManager)\n**Method:** `CheckpointCoordinator.triggerTasks()` \u2192 `Execution.triggerCheckpoint()`\n- For each task in plan, calls `execution.triggerCheckpoint(checkpointId, timestamp, checkpointOptions)`\n- Returns `CompletableFuture<Acknowledge>` for RPC completion\n- Constructs `CheckpointOptions` specifying:\n  - Aligned vs unaligned mode\n  - Checkpoint type (incremental, full)\n  - Aligned checkpoint timeout\n\n### 7. TaskExecutor RPC Reception\n**File:** `flink-runtime/src/main/java/org/apache/flink/runtime/taskexecutor/TaskExecutor.java:triggerCheckpoint()`\n- Receives `taskManagerGateway.triggerCheckpoint()` RPC\n- Looks up Task by ExecutionAttemptID\n- Calls `task.triggerCheckpointBarrier(checkpointId, timestamp, checkpointOptions)`\n\n### 8. Barrier Emission (Source Tasks)\n**Method:** `Task.triggerCheckpointBarrier()` \u2192 `CheckpointableTask.triggerCheckpointAsync()`\n- For StreamTask: routes to `triggerCheckpointAsyncInMailbox()`\n- Creates barrier object with checkpoint ID, timestamp, options\n- For source tasks: injects barrier into output stream immediately\n- For regular operators: waits for barrier arrival from upstream (already injected by sources)\n\n### 9. Barrier Propagation (Network Layer)\n**Components:**\n- Barrier serialized by `EventSerializer.serializeCheckpointBarrier()`\n- Transported through network partition channels\n- Deserialized on receiver side by `EventSerializer.deserializeCheckpointBarrier()`\n\n### 10. Barrier Reception & Alignment (Downstream Tasks)\n**Switch:** Selected based on checkpoint options:\n\n#### **Aligned Path** (SingleCheckpointBarrierHandler)\n- **Method:** `SingleCheckpointBarrierHandler.processBarrier(CheckpointBarrier, InputChannelInfo)`\n- **Behavior:**\n  - Blocks input channels that haven't received barrier yet\n  - Accumulates barriers from all input channels\n  - When all barriers received: notifies task to trigger checkpoint\n  - Unblocks channels to continue processing\n\n#### **Unaligned Path** (CheckpointBarrierTracker)\n- **Method:** `CheckpointBarrierTracker.processBarrier(CheckpointBarrier, InputChannelInfo)`\n- **Behavior:**\n  - Does NOT block channels\n  - Simply counts barriers received for checkpoint ID\n  - When all barriers accounted for: notifies task to trigger checkpoint\n  - Continues processing in-flight data without waiting\n\n### 11. State Snapshot on Barrier\n**Method:** `CheckpointBarrierHandler.notifyCheckpoint()` \u2192 `CheckpointableTask.triggerCheckpointOnBarrier()`\n- Calls `SubtaskCheckpointCoordinator.checkpointState()`\n- Operator snapshots state to backend (RocksDB, memory, etc.)\n- Channel state captured (unaligned) or empty (aligned)\n- Returns `TaskStateSnapshot` with:\n  - OperatorSubtaskState for each operator\n  - InputChannelState (unaligned only)\n  - ResultSubpartitionState (unaligned only)\n\n### 12. Acknowledgment Submission (Task \u2192 JobManager)\n**Flow:** Task state snapshotting completes\n- Calls `environment.acknowledgeCheckpoint(checkpointId, metrics, subtaskState)`\n- Routes to `CheckpointResponder.acknowledgeCheckpoint()`\n- Sends RPC: `checkpointCoordinatorGateway.acknowledgeCheckpoint()`\n- Message type: `AcknowledgeCheckpoint(jobId, executionAttemptId, checkpointId, subtaskState, metrics)`\n\n### 13. Acknowledgment Reception (CheckpointCoordinator)\n**Method:** `CheckpointCoordinator.receiveAcknowledgeMessage(AcknowledgeCheckpoint)`\n- Retrieves PendingCheckpoint by ID\n- Calls `pendingCheckpoint.acknowledgedTasks(executionAttemptId, subtaskState, metrics)`\n- Returns `TaskAcknowledgeResult`:\n  - SUCCESS: increments ack count\n  - DUPLICATE: ignores\n  - UNKNOWN/DISCARDED: discards state handle\n- Checks if checkpoint fully acknowledged: `pendingCheckpoint.isFullyAcknowledged()`\n\n### 14. Checkpoint Completion (Transition to CompletedCheckpoint)\n**Method:** `CheckpointCoordinator.completePendingCheckpoint(PendingCheckpoint)`\n\n**Sub-steps:**\n1. **Finalization:** `pendingCheckpoint.finalizeCheckpoint()`\n   - Serializes checkpoint metadata\n   - Creates `CompletedCheckpoint` with state handles\n\n2. **Store Addition:** `completedCheckpointStore.addCheckpoint(completedCheckpoint)`\n   - Persists metadata to external storage (filesystem, ZK, etc.)\n   - Registers with SharedStateRegistry for cleanup coordination\n\n3. **Subsumption:** Discards older pending checkpoints that are subsumed\n\n4. **Notification:** Sends `AcknowledgeCheckpointRequest` to all tasks\n   - Notifies tasks that checkpoint is committed\n   - Allows garbage collection of in-flight data buffered for unaligned checkpoints\n\n### 15. Post-Completion Cleanup\n**Method:** `CheckpointCoordinator.cleanupAfterCompletedCheckpoint()`\n- Completes future: `pendingCheckpoint.getCompletionFuture().complete(completedCheckpoint)`\n- Triggers statistics reporting\n- Schedules next checkpoint if periodic\n\n---\n\n## Analysis\n\n### Design Patterns Identified\n\n#### 1. **Two-Phase Commit Protocol**\nThe checkpoint mechanism implements a distributed two-phase commit:\n- **Phase 1 (Prepare):** CheckpointCoordinator sends trigger RPC to all tasks\n- **Phase 2 (Commit):** Tasks acknowledge with state handles; when all acknowledge, checkpoint is finalized and committed to external storage\n\n#### 2. **Asynchronous Future-Based Orchestration**\nAll major steps use `CompletableFuture<T>` for non-blocking async composition:\n- Checkpoint plan calculation\n- Storage initialization\n- Operator coordinator snapshots\n- Task acknowledgments\n- Each stage chains via `.thenApplyAsync()` or `.thenComposeAsync()` to serialize across executor/timer threads\n\n#### 3. **Barrier Injection as Snapshot Boundary**\nBarriers embedded in the network stream serve dual purposes:\n- **Semantic boundary:** Mark the boundary between pre-checkpoint and post-checkpoint data\n- **Ordering enforcement:** Ensure all upstream data is flushed before barrier reaches downstream (for aligned checkpoints)\n\n#### 4. **Handler Strategy Pattern**\n`CheckpointBarrierHandler` abstractions encapsulate alignment strategy:\n- **SingleCheckpointBarrierHandler:** Blocks channels (aligned) or unblocks immediately (unaligned)\n- **CheckpointBarrierTracker:** Never blocks (at-least-once semantics)\n- Runtime selects implementation based on `CheckpointOptions.isUnalignedCheckpoint()`\n\n#### 5. **Pending/Completed State Separation**\n- **PendingCheckpoint:** Mutable in-flight checkpoint tracking acknowledgments\n- **CompletedCheckpoint:** Immutable snapshot after all acknowledgments and persistence\n- Transition is atomic via `completePendingCheckpoint()` transition\n\n### Component Responsibilities\n\n#### **CheckpointCoordinator** (flink-runtime/checkpoint/)\n- **Role:** Central JobManager-side orchestrator\n- **Responsibilities:**\n  - Trigger initiation (periodic or on-demand)\n  - Checkpoint plan calculation\n  - PendingCheckpoint lifecycle management\n  - RPC dispatch to TaskExecutor\n  - Acknowledgment collection and validation\n  - Completion and persistence\n  - Statistics tracking and failure handling\n\n#### **PendingCheckpoint** (flink-runtime/checkpoint/)\n- **Role:** In-flight checkpoint state tracker\n- **Responsibilities:**\n  - Track which tasks have acknowledged\n  - Collect and validate state handles from tasks\n  - Implement timeout-based cancellation\n  - Provide completion promise for async notification\n  - Lifecycle: PENDING \u2192 COMPLETED or DISCARDED\n\n#### **Execution** (flink-runtime/executiongraph/)\n- **Role:** Task execution wrapper at JobGraph level\n- **Responsibilities:**\n  - Maintain RPC connection to assigned TaskExecutor\n  - Send `triggerCheckpoint()` RPC with checkpoint metadata\n  - Track RPC acknowledgment futures\n\n#### **Task** (flink-runtime/taskmanager/)\n- **Role:** TaskManager-side task instance\n- **Responsibilities:**\n  - Receive `triggerCheckpointBarrier()` RPC\n  - Route to `CheckpointableTask.triggerCheckpointAsync()`\n  - Handle execution state validation (must be RUNNING)\n  - Reject if not running and invoke `declineCheckpoint()`\n\n#### **StreamTask** (flink-streaming-java/runtime/tasks/)\n- **Role:** Concrete streaming task implementation\n- **Responsibilities:**\n  - Implement `triggerCheckpointAsync()` in mailbox context\n  - Emit checkpoint barriers into output stream\n  - Create `SubtaskCheckpointCoordinator` for state snapshotting\n  - Coordinate with barrier handlers\n\n#### **CheckpointBarrierHandler** (flink-streaming-java/runtime/io/checkpointing/)\n- **Role:** Barrier reception and alignment logic\n- **Responsibilities:**\n  - Receive barriers from input channels\n  - Implement alignment/blocking strategy\n  - Aggregate barrier arrivals\n  - Notify task when checkpoint should be triggered\n  - Measure alignment duration and backpressure\n\n#### **SingleCheckpointBarrierHandler** (flink-streaming-java/runtime/io/checkpointing/)\n- **Role:** Aligned (or optionally unaligned) checkpoint coordination\n- **Responsibilities:**\n  - Manage state machine via `BarrierHandlerState` implementations\n  - Block channels until all barriers received (aligned mode)\n  - Handle barrier timeout and switch to unaligned if needed\n  - Track alignment duration for metrics\n\n#### **CheckpointBarrierTracker** (flink-streaming-java/runtime/io/checkpointing/)\n- **Role:** Non-blocking barrier tracking for at-least-once\n- **Responsibilities:**\n  - Count barrier arrivals without blocking\n  - Trigger checkpoint when all barriers accounted for\n  - Handle checkpoint abortion and subsumption\n\n### Data Flow Description\n\n#### **Trigger Flow (JobManager \u2192 Tasks)**\n```\nCheckpointCoordinator.triggerCheckpoint()\n  \u2193 [allocate checkpoint ID, init storage]\n  createPendingCheckpoint()\n  \u2193 [checkpoint operator coordinators]\n  snapshotMasterState()\n  \u2193 [for each task in plan]\n  Execution.triggerCheckpoint()\n    \u2193 [RPC over TaskManagerGateway]\n    TaskExecutor.triggerCheckpoint()\n      \u2193\n      Task.triggerCheckpointBarrier()\n        \u2193\n        CheckpointableTask.triggerCheckpointAsync()\n          \u2193\n          [StreamTask injects barrier into output stream]\n```\n\n#### **Barrier Flow (Network \u2192 Downstream Tasks)**\n```\n[Source emits CheckpointBarrier]\n  \u2193 [into network output stream, serialized]\n  [Network channels: pipelined or buffered propagation]\n    \u2193\n  [Downstream task receives barrier on InputChannel]\n    \u2193\n    CheckpointBarrierHandler.processBarrier()\n      \u2193 [Aligned: blocks channels, Unaligned: doesn't block]\n      [When all barriers received or timeout]\n      notifyCheckpoint()\n        \u2193\n        CheckpointableTask.triggerCheckpointOnBarrier()\n          \u2193\n          SubtaskCheckpointCoordinator.checkpointState()\n            \u2193 [Snapshot operator state to backend]\n            [Return TaskStateSnapshot with state handles]\n```\n\n#### **Acknowledgment Flow (Tasks \u2192 JobManager)**\n```\n[Task state snapshotting complete]\n  \u2193\n  RuntimeEnvironment.acknowledgeCheckpoint()\n    \u2193\n    CheckpointResponder.acknowledgeCheckpoint()\n      \u2193 [RPC over CheckpointCoordinatorGateway]\n      CheckpointCoordinator.receiveAcknowledgeMessage()\n        \u2193\n        PendingCheckpoint.acknowledgedTasks()\n          \u2193 [Validate, store state handles]\n          [Check if fully acknowledged]\n            \u2193 [If yes]\n            completePendingCheckpoint()\n              \u2193\n              pendingCheckpoint.finalizeCheckpoint()\n              completedCheckpointStore.addCheckpoint()\n              [Notify tasks: CommitCheckpoint message]\n```\n\n### Interface Contracts Between Components\n\n#### **CheckpointCoordinator \u2194 Execution**\n- **Method:** `Execution.triggerCheckpoint(id, timestamp, options)`\n- **Contract:** Return `CompletableFuture<Acknowledge>` indicating RPC delivery\n- **Guarantees:** Asynchronous, may timeout or fail if task not running\n\n#### **Task \u2194 CheckpointableTask**\n- **Method:** `CheckpointableTask.triggerCheckpointAsync(metadata, options)`\n- **Contract:** Return `CompletableFuture<Boolean>` (success/failure)\n- **Guarantees:** Must inject barriers into output in order, must not block indefinitely\n\n#### **CheckpointBarrierHandler \u2194 CheckpointableTask**\n- **Method:** `CheckpointBarrierHandler.processBarrier(barrier, channelInfo, isRpcTriggered)`\n- **Contract:** Synchronous or queued async processing of barriers\n- **Guarantees:** Must eventually call `notifyCheckpoint()` if all barriers arrive, must not lose barriers\n\n#### **CheckpointBarrierHandler \u2194 InputGate**\n- **Method:** Blocking/unblocking of `CheckpointableInput` channels\n- **Contract:** Can block to enforce alignment or unblock for unaligned mode\n- **Guarantees:** Backpressure applied synchronously\n\n#### **Task \u2194 CheckpointResponder**\n- **Method:** `CheckpointResponder.acknowledgeCheckpoint(jobId, executionId, checkpointId, state)`\n- **Contract:** Asynchronous RPC; may be retried on failure\n- **Guarantees:** State handles are serialized, may arrive out of order or duplicate\n\n#### **CheckpointCoordinator \u2194 CompletedCheckpointStore**\n- **Method:** `CompletedCheckpointStore.addCheckpoint(completedCheckpoint)`\n- **Contract:** Synchronous or async persistence to durable storage\n- **Guarantees:** Must be idempotent (handle duplicate additions)\n\n---\n\n## Aligned vs Unaligned Checkpoint Handling\n\n### **Aligned Checkpoints** (default)\n- **SingleCheckpointBarrierHandler implements blocking alignment**\n- **Mechanism:**\n  1. When first barrier arrives, mark alignment start\n  2. Block all input channels immediately\n  3. Buffer or discard any in-flight data arriving after barrier from blocked channels\n  4. When all channels have sent barrier: unblock and trigger checkpoint\n  5. Continue processing from point where all channels are aligned on same checkpoint boundary\n\n- **Guarantees:** Exactly-once processing semantics\n  - All operators see consistent global snapshot\n  - No data loss even on failure (backed by unblocked queues)\n\n- **Trade-off:** Latency increase during alignment\n  - Backpressure propagates upstream\n  - Slow channels can block fast channels\n\n- **Timeout:** If alignment exceeds `alignedCheckpointTimeout`, fall back to unaligned mode\n\n### **Unaligned Checkpoints** (can be forced or fallback)\n- **SingleCheckpointBarrierHandler in unaligned state OR CheckpointBarrierTracker**\n- **Mechanism:**\n  1. Barrier triggers checkpoint immediately upon receipt at first channel\n  2. Do NOT block other channels\n  3. In-flight data from blocked channels is captured as channel state\n  4. Other barriers continue arriving asynchronously\n  5. Checkpoint includes channel state snapshots for all inflight data\n\n- **Guarantees:** At-least-once semantics (without channel state) or exactly-once (with channel state recovery)\n  - Channel state allows recovery of in-flight records that were buffered when failure occurred\n  - No data loss if channel state is included in snapshot\n\n- **Trade-off:** Larger state size (includes in-flight data buffers)\n  - Lower checkpoint latency (no alignment wait)\n  - Faster recovery (no need to replay from last aligned snapshot)\n\n- **Configuration:**\n  - `enableUnalignedCheckpoints()`: Allow fallback to unaligned on timeout\n  - `setForceUnalignedCheckpoints()`: Always use unaligned (no alignment)\n\n---\n\n## PendingCheckpoint Lifecycle\n\n### **State Transitions**\n```\n1. CREATED (constructor)\n   \u2514\u2500 Registers timeout via timer.schedule()\n   \u2514\u2500 Initializes notYetAcknowledgedTasks from CheckpointPlan\n\n2. ACKNOWLEDGED (per task)\n   \u2514\u2500 acknowledgedTasks(executionAttemptID, ...) called per task ack\n   \u2514\u2500 Increments numAcknowledgedTasks\n   \u2514\u2500 Stores OperatorSubtaskState from task\n\n3. FULLY ACKNOWLEDGED (when numAcknowledgedTasks == plan.size())\n   \u2514\u2500 Triggers completePendingCheckpoint()\n   \u2514\u2500 Transitions to DISCARDED (via dispose())\n\n4. DISPOSED\n   \u2514\u2500 discardSubtaskState() clears all stored state handles\n   \u2514\u2500 Cancels timeout\n   \u2514\u2500 finalizeCheckpoint() \u2192 CompletedCheckpoint created or error thrown\n\n5. COMPLETED\n   \u2514\u2500 CompletedCheckpoint persisted to store\n   \u2514\u2500 onCompletionPromise.complete(completedCheckpoint)\n```\n\n### **Timeout Handling**\n- `PendingCheckpoint.cancellerHandle` contains scheduled `ScheduledFuture`\n- If timeout expires before full acknowledgment: `abortPendingCheckpoint(cause)`\n- Triggers: `declineCheckpoint()` RPC to all not-yet-acknowledged tasks\n- Removes from `pendingCheckpoints` map\n\n### **Failure/Abort Path**\n- `CheckpointCoordinator.abortPendingCheckpoint(PendingCheckpoint, reason)`\n- Discards all accumulated state handles via `discardSubtaskState()`\n- Removes pending checkpoint from map\n- Reports failure to failure manager for metric tracking\n\n---\n\n## Summary\n\nThe Flink checkpoint coordination architecture implements a **sophisticated distributed two-phase commit protocol** that achieves fault tolerance through consistent snapshot coordination. The system is built on several key principles:\n\n1. **Barrier-based snapshots:** Checkpoints are marked by special events (barriers) injected into the data stream, ensuring all operators see a consistent boundary between pre- and post-checkpoint data.\n\n2. **Asynchronous pipeline:** Checkpoint triggering, state collection, and acknowledgment flow asynchronously through independent channels (RPC) rather than blocking the main task execution.\n\n3. **Pluggable alignment strategy:** The barrier handler abstraction allows runtime selection between aligned (exactly-once, higher latency) and unaligned (lower latency, larger state) modes.\n\n4. **Pending/completed duality:** In-flight checkpoints (PendingCheckpoint) track acknowledgments independently from finalized snapshots (CompletedCheckpoint), enabling atomic state transitions and reliable recovery guarantees.\n\nThe end-to-end flow spans from checkpoint coordination at the JobManager, through barrier propagation in the network, to state snapshotting and acknowledgment collection at tasks, finally returning to the coordinator for persistent storage\u2014creating a robust, distributed mechanism for periodic application snapshots.\n",

# Flink Checkpoint Coordination Architecture Analysis

## Files Examined

### Core Coordination Components
- **flink-runtime/src/main/java/org/apache/flink/runtime/checkpoint/CheckpointCoordinator.java** — Central JobManager-side coordinator that orchestrates checkpoint triggering, barrier dispatch, state collection, and completion
- **flink-runtime/src/main/java/org/apache/flink/runtime/checkpoint/PendingCheckpoint.java** — Represents an in-flight checkpoint tracking acknowledged tasks and state handles until all acknowledgments arrive
- **flink-runtime/src/main/java/org/apache/flink/runtime/checkpoint/CompletedCheckpoint.java** — Immutable completed checkpoint containing final state handles and metadata

### Barrier Injection & Propagation
- **flink-runtime/src/main/java/org/apache/flink/runtime/io/network/api/CheckpointBarrier.java** — Event object carrying checkpoint ID, timestamp, and options through task network streams
- **flink-runtime/src/main/java/org/apache/flink/runtime/executiongraph/Execution.java** — Execution vertex wrapper that sends RPC triggerCheckpoint() to TaskExecutor
- **flink-runtime/src/main/java/org/apache/flink/runtime/taskmanager/Task.java** — Receives RPC triggerCheckpointBarrier() call and invokes task's triggerCheckpointAsync()

### Barrier Alignment & Processing
- **flink-streaming-java/src/main/java/org/apache/flink/streaming/runtime/io/checkpointing/SingleCheckpointBarrierHandler.java** — Aligned checkpoint handler blocks input channels until all barriers arrive (or unaligned if configured)
- **flink-runtime/src/main/java/org/apache/flink/streaming/runtime/io/checkpointing/CheckpointBarrierTracker.java** — Unaligned checkpoint handler that tracks barriers without blocking channels
- **flink-runtime/src/main/java/org/apache/flink/streami
... (truncated)
